Why	O
is	O

?	O

With	O

A	O

of	O
execution	O
(	O
and	O

,	O
and	O

,	O
not	O
a	O

.	O

Currently	O

warp	O
consists	O
of	O
32	O
threads	O
.	O

This	O
means	O
that	O
all	O
4	O
of	O
your	O
threads	O
per	O
block	O
(	O
since	O
there	O
is	O
no	O
conditional	O
behavior	O
in	O
this	O
case	O
)	O
are	O
executing	O
in	O
lockstep	O
.	O

When	O
they	O
reach	O
the	O
printf	O
function	O
call	O
,	O
they	O
all	O
execute	O
the	O
call	O
to	O
that	O
function	O
in	O

same	O
line	O
of	O
code	O
,	O
in	O
lockstep	O
.	O

So	O
the	O
question	O
becomes	O
,	O
in	O
this	O
situation	O
,	O
how	O
does	O
the	O
CUDA	B-Skill
runtime	O
dispatch	O
these	O
"	O
simultaneous	O
"	O
function	O
calls	O
?	O

to	O
that	O

is	O
unspecified	O
,	O
but	O
it	O
is	O
not	O
"	O
random	O
"	O
.	O

that	O

for	O

from	O
run	O
to	O
run	O
.	O

enough	O
threads	O
to	O

warps	O
per	O
block	O
,	O
and	O
probably	O

include	O

to	O

or	O
"	O

"	O

,	O

to	O

printf	O

emanating	O
from	O
separate	O
warps	O
occurring	O
in	O
"	O

"	O
order	O
.	O

To	O

second	O
part	O
of	O
your	O

,	O

if	O

.	O
